<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таить.html>таи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***так.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> (26)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тако</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tako</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">такъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">takŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tako</i> (adverb), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*takъ</i> (adjective). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">тако</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tako</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; Belarusian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be"><a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; Bulgarian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">така</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; Serbo-Croatian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">тако</i>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh"><a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a></i>; Slovene <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">tаkо</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">tàk</i>; Czech and Polish <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">tak</i>; Upper and Lower Sorbian <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">tak</i>; Lithuanian <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">tóks</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">tokià</i>; and Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tālis</i>. Akin to Old Church Slavonic pronoun <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">тъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a>, определительное, <a href = vnd.unilang:образ.html>образа</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:способ.html>спо́соба</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:действие.html>де́йствия</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:частица.html>части́ца</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:союзный.html>сою́зное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a>; неизменяемое.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-так-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***также.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> (321)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>та́кже</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tákže</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>also, too, as well, likewise
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>та́кже</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:приходить.html>прихо́дит</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>tákže</b> prixódit.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He too is coming.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in negative constructions</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> either, neither, nor</li></ol>

***таки.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:таки.html>таки́</a> (240)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таки.html>таки́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">takí</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>still, after all, in spite of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:таки.html>таки́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поехать.html>пое́хала</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> росси́ю</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oná <b>takí</b> pojéxala v Rossíju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">she went to Russia after all.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:таки.html>таки́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>прав</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>takí</b> ne prav</i> ― <span class="e-translation">still, he is in the wrong.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>May be added after almost any word to add emphasis.
</p>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таки.html>та́ки</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">táki</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span>

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">genitive singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">та́ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">táka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">nominative plural of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">та́ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">táka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>

***талант.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:талант.html>талант</a> (2034)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:талант.html>тала́нт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">talánt</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:талант.html>тала́нта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:талант.html>тала́нты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:талант.html>тала́нтов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>talent, gift
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарывать.html>зарыва́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свой</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:талант.html>тала́нт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>зе́млю</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zaryvátʹ svoj <b>talánt</b> v zémlju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bury one's talent;  to hide one's light under a bushel;  to hide one's talents in a napkin</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> man or woman of talent, gifted person, talent</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> talent <i>(measure of weight and monetary unit)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:талый.html>та́лый</a> (13801)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таять.html>та́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tájatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to melt, thaw</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-таможн-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-я</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тамошний.html>та́мошний</a> (8368)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тамо</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tamo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">there</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-шний</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-šnij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тамошний.html>та́мошний</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">támošnij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> of that place, of those places, local
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тамошний.html>та́мошние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:житель.html>жи́тели</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>támošnije</b> žíteli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the inhabitants there; the inhabitants of that place; locals</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
